function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 419') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.419!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

if (!is_file('3p/_overview')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: 3p/_overview');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('3p/_overview')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/_overview');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/_overview') != '0aec4aecefba0887d5f196129743ce161ac1c5c9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/_overview');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/_overview', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/_overview');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== '0aec4aecefba0887d5f196129743ce161ac1c5c9') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== '82e2399f07039dfd2c0a9dacd7627e286c1b7259') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/_overview');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/_overview');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/_overview')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/_overview', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== '0aec4aecefba0887d5f196129743ce161ac1c5c9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/_overview');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.min.js.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.min.js.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.min.js.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') != 'fa6e4e5d676de8e4bfd2e9e276e8d48588477c1b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.js.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.min.js.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== 'fa6e4e5d676de8e4bfd2e9e276e8d48588477c1b') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== 'e5fb775e481467d46502ada6ddc2636decfac9f6') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.min.js.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.min.js.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== 'fa6e4e5d676de8e4bfd2e9e276e8d48588477c1b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '880a11f5a8e82393f0d6949ec5a427f8cd765e42') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '880a11f5a8e82393f0d6949ec5a427f8cd765e42') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'b5bc0e72c7e3aa61d889a39389205e59a4d1889a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '880a11f5a8e82393f0d6949ec5a427f8cd765e42') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}
